Title: 藪の中

----

Title-ruby: <ruby><rb>藪</rb><rt>やぶ</rt></ruby>の<ruby><rb>中</rb><rt>なか</rt></ruby>

----

Title-english: In a Grove

----

Author: 

<ruby><rb>芥川</rb><rt>あくたがわ</rt></ruby><ruby><rb>龍之介</rb><rt>りゅうのすけ</rt></ruby>

----

Author-english: Akutagawa Ryūnosuke

----

Blurb: For one murder in a bamboo grove there are seven witnesses, but none of them agree.

----

Level: Intermediate

----

Premium: true
